          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/10646544-how-to-flirt-with-a-naked-werewolf">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to ♥Rachel♥ by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/1131400-karlyn-p">♡Karlyn P♡</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5481477-rachel?shelf=audio-book">audio-book</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer830813463" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4206379912973159410"><b>How to Flirt with A Naked Werewolf</b> was a sexy romance filled with quirky characters, and laugh-out-loud moments. Set in a small Alaskan town, this was sort of like Northern Exposure with werewolves. Loved it! <br/><br/>Twenty-nine year old Mo Duvall-Wenstein (I won’t tell you what Mo is short for, but it is funny) moves to Grundy, Alaska to get away from her crazy, hippy parents, Ash and Saffron. Seriously, if these two were my parents, I’d run for the hills, too! So she moves up there to figure out what </span>
  <span id="freeText4206379912973159410" style="display:none"><b>How to Flirt with A Naked Werewolf</b> was a sexy romance filled with quirky characters, and laugh-out-loud moments. Set in a small Alaskan town, this was sort of like Northern Exposure with werewolves. Loved it! <br /><br />Twenty-nine year old Mo Duvall-Wenstein (I won’t tell you what Mo is short for, but it is funny) moves to Grundy, Alaska to get away from her crazy, hippy parents, Ash and Saffron. Seriously, if these two were my parents, I’d run for the hills, too! So she moves up there to figure out what she wants to do with her life without their influence. Mo doesn’t expect to get a job but she ends up in the right place at the right time and becomes the cook for the local hangout, The Blue Glacier Saloon, making friends and gaining admirers along the way. <br /><b><br />Something about the way these men approached me made me think I was being evaluated as breeding stock. <br /><br />However, I think my potential suitors were thinking more along the lines of: <i>Breasts</i> (Check.) <i>Pulse? </i>(Optional, but check.)<br /></b><br />Lol!<br /><br />This is where she meets Cooper, a gorgeous mountain man who organizes and guides parties through the Alaskan wilderness. He’s less than sweet to newcomers, because most don’t last through one winter, and in his opinion Mo will be just like the rest. Cooper is immediately rude to her, so you know as a reader these two are meant to be. Let the sparks fly! However, what you see with Cooper is not all you get, something that Mo is about to find out. When attacks and disappearances rock this little sleepy town, Mo wonders who is responsible and who will be next. <br /><br />This was such a fun, quirky story. I loved the odd characters: Evie, and Buzz, the saloon owners, and all the regular patrons were hilarious! With her outgoing and friendly personality, Mo quickly makes friends and fits in with this bunch. Being away from her parents is the best thing for her, and she finds Grundy is a place she truly belongs, man or no man. Cooper is just the icing on the cake (I wouldn’t mind a piece, thank you!). Sweet, sexy, and a little pushy, but that’s a little inherent with his type *ahem, cough, werewolf*! There was some definite steam in this story!<br /><br /><b>How to Flirt with a Naked Werewolf</b> hooked me from the beginning, and kept my attention long after I finished my commute home. I listened to the audio version and found I didn’t want to shut it off once I walked in the door. This was a consuming combination of mystery, humor, and a hot romance! <br /> </span>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18387313-lleskelle---teams-ren-i-like-big-b00ks?shelf=shapeshifters">shapeshifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18387313-lleskelle---teams-ren-i-like-big-b00ks?shelf=humor">humor</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1939574875" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18151972417193885178">⭐️⭐️⭐️ <b>3 STARS</b> ⭐️⭐️⭐️<br/>I loved the writing and fell in love with the heroine. Mo was all kind of awesome and I completely fell for her and cracked up more than once each time she would share about her upbringing.<br/>I was charmed by the setting of a small town romance, Grundy, Alaska definitely has some perks. <br/><br/>The plot was... predictable. No surprises for me here, but I enjoyed Mo's antics and POV so much, I went with the flow anyway.<br/>The romance was... wonky. I mean, yes the sex scenes were steamy but</span>
  <span id="freeText18151972417193885178" style="display:none">⭐️⭐️⭐️ <b>3 STARS</b> ⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>I loved the writing and fell in love with the heroine. Mo was all kind of awesome and I completely fell for her and cracked up more than once each time she would share about her upbringing.<br>I was charmed by the setting of a small town romance, Grundy, Alaska definitely has some perks. <br><br>The plot was... predictable. No surprises for me here, but I enjoyed Mo's antics and POV so much, I went with the flow anyway.<br>The romance was... wonky. I mean, yes the sex scenes were steamy but the chemistry between Mo and Cooper? Pretty spotty to me. One minute it was there, the next I had no idea where it went. <br><br>The shifter part fell a little short for me though,—very shifter lite— the hero kept giving hasty and generic explanations whenever he was asked about his kind “That's the way of the shifters” and it hardly ever explained anything at all.<br>This was more a chick-lit book borrowing from the shifter pnr genre and it left me craving for a "real" shapeshifter romance.<br><br>I'll probably read the next books in the series, with the hope they run more toward PNR than chick-lit. Nothing wrong with chick-lit, just well a little wrong sided with a title mentioning werewolves and barely anything about them in the book but vague explanations.<br><br><i>

<div id="review_579751456" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/579751456" />
    <a title="Ingie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15589375-ingie"><img alt="Ingie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1477339772p2/15589375.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/579751456?book_show_action=true">Apr 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ingie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ingie" href="/user/show/15589375-ingie">Ingie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Ingie by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/13954899-kathleen">Kathleen</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15589375-ingie?shelf=books-i-read-2013">books-i-read-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15589375-ingie?shelf=romance-m-f-contemporary">romance-m-f-contemporary</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer579751456" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7850886642917680024"><b>4 Stars - well written with funny characters, some steamy sweet love, a naked man (werewolf) and a wonderful dialogue (banters) at best Chick Lit style</b><br/><br/><b>A delight to read</b> - so many wonderful witty comments and thoughts from this exuberant, quick-witted and a survivor and, based on this measurement, also a pretty tough heroine <b>Mo</b>. She is a 30 years old woman, who after a flown boyfriend, nagging parents and a boring job requires a change of scenery, and moves from the warm south to a small cabin in</span>
  <span id="freeText7850886642917680024" style="display:none"><b>4 Stars - well written with funny characters, some steamy sweet love, a naked man (werewolf) and a wonderful dialogue (banters) at best Chick Lit style</b><br><br><b>A delight to read</b> - so many wonderful witty comments and thoughts from this exuberant, quick-witted and a survivor and, based on this measurement, also a pretty tough heroine <b>Mo</b>. She is a 30 years old woman, who after a flown boyfriend, nagging parents and a boring job requires a change of scenery, and moves from the warm south to a small cabin in Alaska.<br><br><b>But what is visible on the outside</b> is not always what's underneath. Yes, and even a quite common, very nice and well behaved girl must have her little secrets:<br><blockquote>'I loved lingerie. I loved the feel of satin and silk on my skin. I loved the juxtaposition of wearing a pair of two-hundred-dollar lace panties under blue jeans, like the pair I was wearing at the moment. Lingerie was a personal statement that you didn't have to declare to the world. You could be as demure or as naughty as you wanted to be, and no one ever had to know unless you showed them... or were injured in a serious car accident.'</blockquote><br><b>Mo (or whatever her long impressed hippie name is) soon gets a slightly grumpy</b> - big, huge, strong but somethimes fragile - Alpha Male, a <i>Living.in.the.Forest</i> kind of hero, called <b>Cooper</b> in her life. A very manly man who prefers to be completely naked - or a guarding but so cuddly wolf. <br><blockquote>‘When a naked man shows up on porch with a bear trap clamped around his ankle, it's best to do what he asks’<br><br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Hearts/image_zps98d29ea9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380416093i/821672.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps98d29ea9.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a>
</blockquote><br><b>What is more warm in the cold North</b> than getting knocked around in bed, on the floor, in the car - yes everywhere with your horny werewolf. All in the little town called Grundy in a freezing cold Alaska ~ but so warm on the inside. <br><br>There is of course a sweet love story here, a love story that took some time before it was on, and I waited patiently for that first kiss. Once it came then took it off in good speed. But this is more a <b>funny novel</b> about this heroine and what happens in her life for a year, than a pure romance. But romantic is it anyway!<br><br><b>Not to forget are all these wonderful second characters</b>, crazy hippie parents, flirting bar guests and about a new-found passion to cook and bake yummy cakes. I just want to give them all a big hug and be there in the snow and cold with all of them. And it's not a little to be desired when you already, like me, experiencing snow and ice biting cold so many days every year. <br><br><b>
  <i>I loved it all...</i>
</b><br><br><blockquote>
<br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Couple%20in%20love/image_zpsdbbe1a5e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380416093i/821673.jpg" alt=" photo image_zpsdbbe1a5e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>‘Maybe it was just an over abundance of hormones, a response to a sexual starvation diet. I'd been without for so long that my body was craving the worst possible thing for me. Cooper was carnal triple chocolate cheesecake, deep-fried on a stick.’</blockquote><br><b>Although you would never otherwise</b> get you to read a book where there are actually a real live werewolf, you can unconditionally read this one. This is not a traditional PNR book. The whole thing with a werewolf boyfriend/lover is just a extra fun sting to the story. Sure it's a little werewolf romance here, but not in some mysterious and adventurous tough and beastly way. Becoming someone's <i>mate</i> here, just feels cozy and sweet and doesn't change the feeling of reading a pretty idyllic small town.<br><br><b>A great romantic, funny and so sweet</b> Chick Lit with some very light, and mainly comic, paranormal in it - A great feelgood read!! To recommend for a fun and entertaining read.<br><br><b>I LIKE - and laughs!! </b><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="7850886642917680024" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_912344503" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/912344503" />
    <a title="Carole (Carole&#39;s Random Life in Books)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books"><img alt="Carole (Carole&#39;s Random Life in Books)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1415550632p2/5892196.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/912344503?book_show_action=true">Jul 12, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carole (Carole&#39;s Random Life in Books)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carole (Carole&#39;s Random Life in Books)" href="/user/show/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books">Carole (Carole&#39;s Random Life in Books)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/10646544-how-to-flirt-with-a-naked-werewolf">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books?shelf=audio-book">audio-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books?shelf=2017">2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer912344503" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14790366034920011155">This review can also be found at <a href='http://carolesrandomlife.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Carole's Random Life in Books</a>.<br/><br/>I could kick myself. I bought this audiobook back in 2015. Heck, I bought the whole series and then promptly got distracted by some other shiny book. I have seen so many great reviews for this book but did I start listening. Nope. Because I was distracted. Well, I finally dusted it off and started listening to it earlier this week and had a great time with it. <br/><br/>Mo is the focus of this story and I liked her character right away. The bo</span>
  <span id="freeText14790366034920011155" style="display:none">This review can also be found at <a href="http://carolesrandomlife.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Carole's Random Life in Books</a>.<br /><br />I could kick myself. I bought this audiobook back in 2015. Heck, I bought the whole series and then promptly got distracted by some other shiny book. I have seen so many great reviews for this book but did I start listening. Nope. Because I was distracted. Well, I finally dusted it off and started listening to it earlier this week and had a great time with it. <br /><br />Mo is the focus of this story and I liked her character right away. The book opens with Mo moving to Alaska. It is a big change from what she is used to in Mississippi but she needs a change. And she needs to get away from her over the top parents. Her parents are quite the pair and I can completely understand why she took such a drastic step. <br /><br />Mo quickly becomes a part of the local community by working at the local bar and grill. She is making friends and finding her way. She is even getting the attention of a couple of the local men. Enter Cooper, local werewolf extraordinaire. Cooper always seems a little grouchy but Mo can't seem to stay away. One thing leads to another and they decide to act on their chemistry. <br /><br />There were so many things to love about this book. I really liked the humor woven into the story. I had a big grin on my face the entire time I was listening to this story. I liked Mo and Cooper as a couple and thought they had great chemistry. The story had a lot of things going on besides the romance with a wolf attacking the local community and some drama with Cooper's family. <br /><br />I really enjoyed Amanda Ronconi's narration. I thought she captured Mo's personality very well through her narration. She handled all of the different characters very well and it was always very easy to tell who was speaking. This story has a wide range of emotions and she portrayed them all very well. I felt Mo's fear, her joy, her confusion, and her frustration. She read the story at a very natural pace and I really just felt like she was telling me a story. I was able to listen to this book for hours at a time and look forward to listening to more of her work in the future.<br /><br />I would recommend this book to fans of paranormal romance. This was a fun story filled with great chemistry and a wonderful sense of humor. This is the first book by Molly Harper that I have read and I cannot wait to continue with this series.<br /><br /><b>Initial Thoughts</b><br />This was fun. There were quite a few funny moments and I really enjoyed Mo's sense of humor. The narration was great and I look forward to listening to more of this series very soon.<br /><br />Book source: Audible purchase</span>
  <a data-text-id="14790366034920011155" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_514072702" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/514072702" />
    <a title="Keertana" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7584700-keertana"><img alt="Keertana" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1438801223p2/7584700.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/514072702?book_show_action=true">Jan 22, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Keertana" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Keertana" href="/user/show/7584700-keertana">Keertana</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Keertana by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/5812324-heidi">Heidi</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7584700-keertana?shelf=swoooon">swoooon</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7584700-keertana?shelf=rainy-day-re-reads">rainy-day-re-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7584700-keertana?shelf=2013-favorites">2013-favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer514072702" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18417899210949889038">Rating: 4.5 Stars<br/><br/>I feel like I always pick up a paranormal adult romance novel thinking that I cannot possibly give it more than three stars and sometimes, I just do. It's not that these books are thought-provoking or deep, it's not that they make you cry or scream, it's not even that they are books that change your life. Instead, they're novels that offer some perfect fun and put a smile on your face when you're down and sometimes, that's even harder to do than write a story that touches your h</span>
  <span id="freeText18417899210949889038" style="display:none">Rating: 4.5 Stars<br /><br />I feel like I always pick up a paranormal adult romance novel thinking that I cannot possibly give it more than three stars and sometimes, I just do. It's not that these books are thought-provoking or deep, it's not that they make you cry or scream, it's not even that they are books that change your life. Instead, they're novels that offer some perfect fun and put a smile on your face when you're down and sometimes, that's even harder to do than write a story that touches your heart. Well, sometimes. <br /><br /><i>How to Flirt with a Naked Werewolf</i> is every bit as funny, romantic, and cute as its title and cover promise. It all starts out when Mo moves hundreds of miles from her humid hometown of Mississippi to Alaska, hoping to re-invent herself. All her life, Mo has been surrounded by completely hipster parents who force her to eat organic food and consider it blasphemous to shop at Wal-Mart. Now, after twenty-nine years of their overbearing presence, Mo has realized that she no longer knows what parts of her are <i>her</i> from what parts of her are simply the person she's become while rebelling against her parents. <br /><br />Thus, a spontaneous move to Alaska ensues. Alaskans, however, aren't overly friendly to strangers, firmly looking down upon folks who move to the wilderness hoping to re-connect with a hidden part of themselves. Grundy, the small town Mo moves into, however, quickly accepts her. Or rather her fantastic cooking. Cooper, the surly neighbor, handsome man, and cousin of the woman who owns the restaurant Mo works in now, though, isn't so taken with Mo. Not only are the two of them constantly at each others throats, but the next thing you know, Mo knows Cooper's secret: he's a werewolf. At a time when people in Grundy are mysteriously being killed by wolves, that's one secret you <i>want</i> to keep. <br /><br />What makes <i>How to Flirt with a Naked Werewolf</i> such a success, for me at least, is Mo. Even from the first page, Mo has a vivacious and compelling personality, full of spunk and courage. Not only is she strong and stubborn, but her narration is absolutely hilarious. Her memories of her childhood are sprinkled with an incredulousness that is somehow believable and the manner in which she so fully integrates herself into Alaskan society is admirable. Even better, she's not afraid to stand up for herself and refuses to take crap from anyone. In other words, she is the perfect type of literary heroine. <br /><br />Enter: Cooper. Cooper reminded me a lot of Mr. Darcy in the beginning of this novel - antisocial, aloof, and grumpy. Yet, what I loved about this book is the phenomenal transformation he slowly makes as the book progresses. Cooper and Mo have a charged relationship from the start and seeing their romance culminate is both rewarding and steamy. Mo evidently has a huge influence on Cooper, but it is not immediate. Cooper is a very multi-layered and intriguing character and peeling back each one of those layers is what kept me riveted to this story, unable to set it down. I literally read it in one sitting, so be prepared to not move for a few hours if you pick this one up. <br /><br />In addition to a toe-curling romance and engaging protagonists, we have a mystery on our hands as well. Since a wolf is running free, killing tourists and villagers in Grundy, Mo's thoughts can't help but flee to Cooper and his family not far away. What I enjoyed about this mystery was that it was perfectly paced, with just the right amount of red herrings to make it obvious, but only if you really, <i>really</i> looked. It still came as a surprise to me by the end and the manner in which it was woven into the romance, making it deeper by the end, was rewarding as well. Even better, the mystery aspect opened new doors for complex family relationships as we got to meet Cooper's parents, sister, and cousins, as well as gain insight into why he, as an alpha, is no longer leading his pack. <br /><br /><i>How to Flirt With a Naked Werewolf</i> is the <i>perfect</i> winter read. It is heartwarming, amusing, and is sure to put a smile on your face and keep it there. Furthermore, its characters are utterly charming and the friendships, romances, and other bonds in this novel will make you form your own ties with these memorable personalities. Mo and Cooper are one of the best paranormal romance couples I've read about and the manner in which their relationship progresses, along with the pacing, is simply perfect. We have character growth, butterfly-inducing romance, and complex relationships, all with a dash of drama, murder mystery, and - let's not forget - sexy werewolves. If that isn't a recipe for success, then I don't know what is. <br /><br />You can read <a href="http://ivybookbindings.blogspot.com/2013/02/review-how-to-flirt-with-naked-werewolf.html" rel="nofollow noopener">this review</a> and more on my blog, <a href="http://ivybookbindings.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Ivy Book Bindings.</a> </span>
  <a data-text-id="18417899210949889038" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1700772943" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1700772943" />
    <a title="Briar&#39;s Reviews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/32054036-briar-s-reviews"><img alt="Briar&#39;s Reviews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1402183274p2/32054036.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1700772943?book_show_action=true">May 05, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Briar&#39;s Reviews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Briar&#39;s Reviews" href="/user/show/32054036-briar-s-reviews">Briar&#39;s Reviews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32054036-briar-s-reviews?shelf=chick-lit">chick-lit</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32054036-briar-s-reviews?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32054036-briar-s-reviews?shelf=cute">cute</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32054036-briar-s-reviews?shelf=drama">drama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32054036-briar-s-reviews?shelf=fiction">fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32054036-briar-s-reviews?shelf=guilty-pleasure">guilty-pleasure</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32054036-briar-s-reviews?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32054036-briar-s-reviews?shelf=top-books">top-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32054036-briar-s-reviews?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32054036-briar-s-reviews?shelf=fantasy-supernatural">fantasy-supernatural</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1700772943" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13537107474800949678">I accidentally stumbled across this book as a local discount store and the cover instantly caught my eye. I kept eying this book down, knowing full well I needed to pick it up, and I finally caved. To no one's surprise, I have been eying this cutesy romance on my book shelf for AGES and I finally knew it was time to pick it up. Nothing is better than my guilty pleasure - romances with a pinch of fantasy!<br/><br/>How to Flirt with a Naked Werewolf follows our lead Mo when she moves to a distant, small tow</span>
  <span id="freeText13537107474800949678" style="display:none">I accidentally stumbled across this book as a local discount store and the cover instantly caught my eye. I kept eying this book down, knowing full well I needed to pick it up, and I finally caved. To no one's surprise, I have been eying this cutesy romance on my book shelf for AGES and I finally knew it was time to pick it up. Nothing is better than my guilty pleasure - romances with a pinch of fantasy!<br /><br />How to Flirt with a Naked Werewolf follows our lead Mo when she moves to a distant, small town in Alaska. She wants to get away from her parents overly obsessive nature of basically controlling her life. It's like this move was meant to be, because suddenly she has friends and a job, and a hot man chasing after her. One day, sexy Cooper wakes up naked on her door step, and guess what? He's the naked werewolf! But is he the werewolf/creature killing the people showing up dead in their town? Mo and Cooper will have to investigate. Will their relationship survive? You'll need to read to find out...<br /><br />This book was super funny and an absolute delight. I felt myself sinking into this book and disappeared until I have binged the whole thing. It really is a lovely, HEA type romance with just enough fantasy and paranormal in it to make it interesting. I really enjoyed watching Mo develop relationships and finally fit in somewhere. It's what every reader seems to want - just to fit in - so it was easy to relate to her. I really liked Mo's arc and that quite a few characters developed over time and became more likable. Also, Mo is thirty years old! Do you know how great it is to see a romance book where the character is an actual ADULT who doesn't have her life figured out yet? RELATABLE. SUPER RELATABLE. THANK YOU!<br /><br />Cooper is a more rough character and maybe not the most romantic of men, but I didn't care. I was more focused on the fun Mo was having and the amazing sex scenes those two were romping in. This book is also a wee bit predictable, but that's what I like in my guilty pleasure reads. Anywho, it seems like every plot has been done to death anyways. <br /><br />There was a few "rougher" parts of this book - brutal death of a character who deserved some bad things to him, and a really sad loss - but other than that it's a great contemporary, paranormal romance. I honestly don't see anything bad with it because any "issues" that were there were so minor it didn't matter. Sooner or later, I will need to find the remaining books in this series and binge it. Molly Harper is gearing up to be one of my new fave authors.<br /><br />Overall, I loved this book! It's sweet, light, full of romance, funny, mushy, sexy and just a great all around read!<br /><br />Four out of five stars.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13537107474800949678" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">

<div id="review_437471808" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/437471808" />
    <a title="Heather K (dentist in my spare time)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time"><img alt="Heather K (dentist in my spare time)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1365526640p2/13070326.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/437471808?book_show_action=true">Oct 19, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Heather K (dentist in my spare time)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Heather K (dentist in my spare time)" href="/user/show/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time">Heather K (dentist in my spare time)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/10646544-how-to-flirt-with-a-naked-werewolf">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=m-f">m-f</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=chick-lit-women-s-fiction">chick-lit-women-s-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=shifters">shifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=narrator-very-good">narrator-very-good</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer437471808" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13069246122796509714"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472750173i/20237706._SX540_.jpg' width='200' height='150' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>**3.5 stars**<br/><br/>This was a fun audiobook. Amanda Ronconi did a spot-on narration of the character of Mo and provided a nice range of distinct voices, even if her male voices sounded like hoarse, slightly constipated females. <br/><br/>The paranormal aspect of this book was pretty light with much of the interesting action focusing on Mo's journey and experiences in Grundy, Alaska. I loved the setting of the small-town Alaskan village and the characters that inhabit the town. The whole ambiance of the book was</span>
  <span id="freeText13069246122796509714" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472750173i/20237706._SX540_.jpg" width="200" height="150" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>**3.5 stars**<br><br>This was a fun audiobook. Amanda Ronconi did a spot-on narration of the character of Mo and provided a nice range of distinct voices, even if her male voices sounded like hoarse, slightly constipated females. <br><br>The paranormal aspect of this book was pretty light with much of the interesting action focusing on Mo's journey and experiences in Grundy, Alaska. I loved the setting of the small-town Alaskan village and the characters that inhabit the town. The whole ambiance of the book was really well done and I immediately got into the groove of the story. <br><br>I also had an excellent time being inside of the head of Mo, who is spunky, self-sufficient, and adorable. I wasn't as enamored with Cooper. I thought that his character was inconsistent. One minute he was surly, the next he was everyone's best friend. I also didn't like the way he ran away from all of his problems and left Mo in the lurch. The good thing was that Mo called him on all of his bull behavior, but I wasn't 100% feeling them as a couple because of my gripes with Cooper. <br><br>All in all, this was a very enjoyable, easy listen and a great way to pass the time on my commute. </span>

          </span>

<div id="review_464177759" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/464177759" />
    <a title="Kathleen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13954899-kathleen"><img alt="Kathleen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1365166675p2/13954899.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/464177759?book_show_action=true">Nov 26, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kathleen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kathleen" href="/user/show/13954899-kathleen">Kathleen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/10456371-how-to-flirt-with-a-naked-werewolf">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13954899-kathleen?shelf=fantastical-romance">fantastical-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13954899-kathleen?shelf=series-opener">series-opener</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer464177759" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14893270172121742754">I liked this! It's a cross between chick-lit and PNR. I chuckled several times (but it's not always lighthearted). It's alternatively witty, sexy, sad, gritty, and suspenseful, with a wonderful cast of secondary characters and a fun sense of community. The ending chapters were a bit grim, and had a slightly different feel..<br/><br/>PLOT with NO MAJOR SPOILERS : Mo (her full name is such a kick!!) moves all the way from Mississippi to Grundy, Alaska to escape her meddling hippie parents. Cooper moves acro</span>
  <span id="freeText14893270172121742754" style="display:none">I liked this! It's a cross between chick-lit and PNR. I chuckled several times (but it's not always lighthearted). It's alternatively witty, sexy, sad, gritty, and suspenseful, with a wonderful cast of secondary characters and a fun sense of community. The ending chapters were a bit grim, and had a slightly different feel..<br /><br />PLOT with NO MAJOR SPOILERS : Mo (her full name is such a kick!!) moves all the way from Mississippi to Grundy, Alaska to escape her meddling hippie parents. Cooper moves across Alaska to escape his memories and his family. Mo is 30 years old, single, "fairly attractive," a great cook, and addicted to lacy La Perla underthings. She instantly gets the hots for Cooper, a gorgeously ripped wilderness guide. He is hot for Mo, too, but is always so growly and grumpy that she looks instead toward the forest ranger, Alan, for companionship. (With a male-female ratio of 20 to 1, she's got her pick, but most are old farts.) Mo and Cooper dance around their mutual attraction for about 1/3 of the book -- there's some banter and repartee as the sexual tension climbs. In several serious scenes, a mysterious black wolf is seen in town. Some of the locals are attacked by a wolf. (Some sadness, a bit grim, some tense scenes.) The plot also revolves around various members of Cooper's family, especially his sister Maggie.<br /><br />SUSPENSE: I didn't figure out who the killer was until well into the book. No give-aways, but some clues along the way. Some red herrings, too.<br /><br />CHARACTERIZATION: Good character development. I grew to care for the variety of old timers who hung out at the Glacier restaurant in Grundy, where our girl Mo works as the new short order cook. I chuckled as Mo became accustomed to salmon, snow, and small town insulated society. Loved how she formed relationships at the café. At first I wasn't too nuts about Cooper, but once he gave in to the attraction....yummy.<br /><br />LOVEMAKING: The first love scene takes place about 1/2 into the book. It's hot. Cooper has a magic mighty morphin penis -- yup, that's what she wrote -- and ninja werewolf sperm. Mo has a bulk box of 100 condoms. What more can I say? Several sexy scenes by the fire, in bed, etc. Cuddling, kissing, nipping, licking...<br /><br />VOICE and STYLE: First person POV. Humorous, with a dry wit. Fairly light, but some scenes are handled seriously. Lots of references to popular culture (ninja, Bill O'Reilly, the B52s, La Perla lingerie, etc.). Some F-bombs and religious swear words -- could do without that -- but not a lot of cussing. Some grizzly stuff, but not too bad. Not nearly as bloody as the UF books by Patty Briggs or Ilona Andrews.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14893270172121742754" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('oRg0foDUm376yOiEl2ww6CujlU160LM9JnYkY32HJk6VjiUp9ZJWQHEeNaBKFv3Bw+lveXbtsDkc17oFvP1BXQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('+O1afAoZpx43zzaGLKKmS6PDfm4YLBHl3USZBAfvUJ3Me0srf19qILwZ66Lx2GtiS4mEWhQREuHn5QdixpU3jg==')})
  }

      <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/2503028.Molly_Harper">About Molly Harper</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/2503028.Molly_Harper"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1263196898p3/2503028.jpg);'></div>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__name'>
<a href="/author/show/2503028.Molly_Harper">Molly Harper

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer7515780619784154891">My mother remembers an 8-year-old me setting up my “writing office” in our living room by putting her old manual typewriter on the couch next to a toy phone. And I (very slowly) pecked out the story of my third-grade class taking a trip around the world and losing a kid in each city.<br/><br/>I had a dark sense of humor, even then.<br/><br/>In high school, when other girls my age were writing poems about dying unicor</span>
  <span id="freeText7515780619784154891" style="display:none">My mother remembers an 8-year-old me setting up my “writing office” in our living room by putting her old manual typewriter on the couch next to a toy phone. And I (very slowly) pecked out the story of my third-grade class taking a trip around the world and losing a kid in each city.<br /><br />I had a dark sense of humor, even then.<br /><br />In high school, when other girls my age were writing poems about dying unicorns and bleeding roses, I was writing essays about having political arguments with my dad at the dinner table. (Whoever made the other person laugh at their own political party won the argument.) I knew I wanted to write when I grew up, but I also knew there was very little chance I could make a living writing books, so I went for the next best thing – newspaper writing. <br /><br />I majored in print journalism at Western Kentucky University and used my shiny new degree to get a job at my hometown newspaper. I married my high school sweetheart, David, a local police officer. And for six years, I wrote about school board meetings, quilt shows, a man “losing” the fully grown bear he kept as a pet in his basement, and a guy who faked his death by shark attack in Florida and ended up tossing pies at a local pizzeria. <br /><br />I loved my job at the paper. I loved meeting new people every day and never knowing where I would end up. But somehow, the ever-shifting schedules of a police officer and a reporter did not equal "family friendly." One of us needed to take a normal job for the sake of our young daughter. I took a secretarial position at a local church office, which left me with dependably free evenings for the first time in my adult life. David was working the night shift that summer and I was losing.my.mind. We were living in "The Apartment of Lost Souls" while building our new home. This was the place where appliances and small electronics went to die. Every night I would tuck our snoozing child into bed and wait for the washing machine to start smoking or the computer to suddenly flash the "blue screen of death." Then there was the plague of frogs in the bathroom that put our daughter of potty-training for about six months.<br /><br />Normally, when things get tough, I can take solace in reading. But I surveyed my packing box of favorite books with the apathetic air of someone who stands in front of the open refrigerator for 10 minutes and can't find anything. Nothing sounded good. So I just sat down and started writing something I would want to read. <br /><br />Being a huge fan of vampire movies and TV shows, I wondered, what would be the most humiliating way possible to be turned into a vampire- a story that a vampire would be embarrassed to share with their vampire buddies over a nice glass of Type O. Well, first, you'd have to make the protaganist a bit of an accidental loser. She's single, almost 30, and a librarian working in the small Kentucky town where she grew up. This "triple whammy of worry" has made her a permanent fixture on her Mama's prayer list. And despite the fact that's pretty good at her job, she just got canned so her boss could replace her with someone who occasionally starts workplace fires. She drowns her sorrows at the local faux nostalgia-themed sports bar and during the commute home, she's mistaken for a deer and then shot by a drunk hunter. And then she wakes up as a vampire.<br /><br />And thus, Jane Jameson and the wacky denizens of Half-Moon Hollow were born.<br /><br />It took me almost a year to complete and edit a draft of the book, which I planned as the first in a three-book series. I spent three months using agentquery.com to ruthlessly stalk potential literary agents. (There were a lot of lists involved, I don't want to re-live it.) I was gently rejected by at least half of them. I corresponded with some very nice, very patient people, but ultimately signed with the fabulous Stephany Evans of Fine Print Literary Management. Stephany was willing to take to the time to give me advice on how to imp</span>
  <a data-text-id="7515780619784154891" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
